    　　　　　忧恚无言篇

    　　舌者，音声之机也。
    　　足之少阴上系于舌，络于横骨，终于会厌。[6p]

    Five Readings and Five Uses

    The tongue is the organ of the heart.
    (Note: The heart opens through the tongue, hence the tongue is considered the organ of the heart.)

    Pulse and Measurement

    The spleen's qi connects to the mouth; when the spleen is harmonious, the mouth can discern the five grains. The heart's qi connects to the tongue; when the heart is harmonious, the tongue can recognize the five flavors.
    (Note: The mouth can distinguish the five grains, and the tongue can identify the five flavors. When the heart and spleen are harmonized, both the mouth and tongue will be in balance, thus the five grains and five flavors can be recognized upon entering.)

    Nourishing and Defensive Qi

    The upper jiao arises from the mouth above the stomach, extending above the throat, penetrating the diaphragm and spreading throughout the chest. It traverses the armpits, follows the pathway of the greater yin, and returns to yangming, rising to the tongue and descending to the lower yangming.
    (Note: The upper jiao that emerges from above the stomach is its connected deployment, extending above the throat, passing through the diaphragm, spreading through the chest, exiting under the armpits, following the pathway of the greater yin, moving back to the yangming’s celestial cauldron, rising to the tongue and then descending to the lower yangming region.)

    Defensive Qi

    The marker of the foot’s lesser yin is located at the back point and the two vessels below the tongue. The marker of the foot’s greater yin is at the back point and the root of the tongue.

    Unspoken Distress and Anger

    The tongue is the mechanism of sound.
    The lesser yin of the foot is connected to the tongue, linking to the transverse bone, and culminating at the epiglottis.[6p]

    　　　　　口问篇

    　　黄帝曰：人之自啮舌者，何气使然？岐伯曰：此厥逆走上，脉气辈至也。少阴气至则啮舌，少阳气至则啮颊，阳明气至则啮唇矣。视主病者则补之。　　 【注　齿者，肾气之所生也。少阴之脉挟舌本，少阳之脉循于颊，如肾之脏生气厥逆走上，与中焦所生之脉气相辈而至，则啮舌。】
    　　　　　肠胃篇

    　　舌重十两，长七寸，广二寸半。

    　　　　金匮要略 【汉　张机】

    　　　　　胎黄

    　　病者腹满，按之不痛为虚，痛者为实，可下之。舌黄，未下者，下之黄自去。　　腹满，舌萎黄，躁不得睡，属黄家。
    　　　　　邪入脏则难言

    　　寸口脉浮而紧，紧则为寒，浮则为虚。寒虚相搏，邪在皮肤。浮者血虚，络脉空虚，贼邪不泻，或左或右。邪气反缓，正气即急。正气引邪，喎僻不遂。邪在于络，肌肤不仁。邪在于经，即重不胜。邪入于腑，即不识人。邪入于脏，舌即难言，口吐涎。[7p]

    Oral Inquiry Chapter

    The Yellow Emperor asked: What energy causes a person to bite their tongue? Qi Bo replied: This is due to the reversed movement upwards; the pulse energy arrives in succession. When the Lesser Yin energy arrives, it causes tongue biting; when the Lesser Yang energy arrives, it causes cheek biting; when the Yang Ming energy arrives, it causes lip biting. Examine the patient to provide nourishment.

    [Note: The teeth are born of kidney energy. The pulse of the Lesser Yin lies at the root of the tongue, while the pulse of the Lesser Yang runs along the cheeks. Just as the energy from the kidneys rises due to reverse movement, it converges with the pulse energy generated from the middle jiao, resulting in tongue biting.]

    Intestines and Stomach Chapter

    The tongue weighs ten taels, measures seven inches in length, and two and a half inches in width.

    ** Essentials of the Golden Coffer [Han Dynasty, Zhang Ji]**

    Fetal Jaundice

    When the patient has abdominal distention, if pressing it does not cause pain, it indicates deficiency; if it causes pain, it indicates excess and can be purged. The tongue appears yellow; if it is not purged, the yellow will naturally dissipate. Abdominal distention, with a wilted yellow tongue and restlessness that prevents sleep, pertains to the yellow family.

    Evil Enters the Organs and is Difficult to Speak of

    The pulse at the inch position is floating and tight; tightness indicates cold, while floating indicates deficiency. When cold and deficiency clash, the evil resides in the skin. If the pulse is floating, it suggests blood deficiency, and the collateral vessels are empty; the invader does not disperse, either left or right. If the evil energy becomes sluggish, the righteous energy quickens. The righteous energy draws the evil, making it difficult to flow smoothly. If the evil is in the collaterals, the skin lacks sensation. If the evil is in the channels, the weight is unbearable. If the evil enters the bowels, one becomes unrecognizable. If the evil enters the organs, it causes difficulties in speech and leads to salivation.[7p]

    　　　　　干燥

    　　肝中寒者，两臂不举，舌本燥，喜太息，胸中痛不得转侧，食则吐而汗出也。　　腹满口舌干燥，此肠间有水气，己椒苈黄圆主之。　　消渴病，渴欲饮水，口干舌燥者，白虎加人参汤主之。　　病人胸满唇委，舌青口燥，但欲漱水不欲咽，无寒热，脉微大来迟，腹不满，其人言我满，为有瘀血。
    　　　　伤寒论 【汉　张机】

    　　　　　干燥

    　　太阳病，重发汗而复下之，不大便五六日，舌上燥而渴，日晡时小有潮热，从心下至少腹，鞕满而痛不可近者，大陷胸汤主之。　　伤寒病，若吐若下后，七八日不解，热结在里，表里俱热，时时恶风，大渴，舌上干燥而烦，欲饮水数升者，白虎加人参汤主之。[8p]

    Dryness

    Cold in the liver causes inability to lift the arms, a dry tongue, a tendency to sigh, chest pain that cannot be alleviated by changing positions, and vomiting along with sweating after eating. Abdominal fullness and dry mouth and tongue indicate water qi in the intestines, treated with the formula of Jiao Li Huang Yuan. For thirst disease, craving water, and a dry mouth and tongue, it is treated with Bai Hu Jia Ren Shen Tang. If a patient experiences fullness in the chest and swollen lips, a blue tongue and dry mouth, desiring only to rinse with water but not to swallow, with no chills or fever, a weak and delayed pulse, and a non-distended abdomen, the person may feel full due to blood stasis.

    On Cold Damage 【Han Zhang Ji】

    Dryness

    For Taiyang disease, excessive sweating followed by purging, resulting in no bowel movement for five or six days, a dry tongue and thirst, and slight fever in the afternoon, with fullness and pain in the chest and hypogastrium that is tender to touch, it is treated with Da Xian Zhong Tang. In cases of cold damage with either vomiting or purging, if after seven to eight days there is no resolution, indicating heat accumulation inside, both surface and interior are hot, with periodic aversion to wind, extreme thirst, dryness on the tongue and irritability, desiring to drink several liters of water, it is treated with Bai Hu Jia Ren Shen Tang.[8p]

    　　　　　白胎

    　　阳明病，胁下鞕满，不大便而呕，舌上白胎者，可与小柴胡汤。上焦得通，津液得下，胃气因和，身濈然而汗出解也。　　病如结胸状，饮食如故，时时下利，寸脉浮，关脉小细沉紧，名曰脏结。舌上白胎滑者，难治。　　脏结无阳证，不往来寒热，其人反静，舌上胎滑者，不可攻也。
    　　　　千金方 【唐　孙思邈】

    　　　　　舌论

    　　凡舌者，心主小肠之候也。舌重十两，长七寸，广二寸半，善用机衡，能调五味也。凡有所啖，若多食咸，则舌脉凝而变色；多食苦，则舌皮槁而外毛焦枯；多食辛，则舌筋急而爪枯干；多食酸，则舌肉肥而唇揭；多食甘，则舌根痛而外发落。又曰心欲苦，肺欲辛，肝欲酸，脾欲甘，肾欲咸，此五味内合五脏之气也。若脏热，则舌生疮，引唇揭赤；若腑寒，则舌本缩，口噤唇青。寒宜补之，热宜泻之，不寒不热，依脏腑调之。舌缩口噤唇青，升麻煎主之。[9p]

    White Coating

    For Yangming disease, if there is fullness beneath the ribs, no bowel movement, and vomiting with a white coating on the tongue, one may administer Xiao Chai Hu Decoction. When the upper burner is unblocked, the fluids descend, and the stomach qi harmonizes, the body will then sweat lightly and ease the condition. If the illness resembles chest binding and the appetite is normal with occasional diarrhea, while the cun pulse is floating and the guan pulse is small, thin, and tight, it is termed 'Zang Jie' (Organ Binding). If the white coating on the tongue is slippery, it is difficult to treat. If Zang Jie presents without yang symptoms, showing no alternation of cold and heat, and the person remains still with a slippery tongue coating, it should not be attacked.

    Tongue Treatise

    The tongue reflects the heart and the status of the small intestine. A tongue weighs ten ounces, measures seven inches in length, and two and a half inches in width. It is adept at assessing and can balance the five flavors. When eating, if one consumes too much salt, the tongue pulse becomes congealed and discolored; too much bitterness leads to a dry appearance of the tongue's surface; too much spiciness causes the tongue muscles to tighten and the edges to become dry; too much sourness makes the tongue flesh swell and the lips reveal; too much sweetness results in pain at the root of the tongue and loss of its outer surface. It is noted that the heart desires bitterness, the lungs desire spiciness, the liver desires sourness, the spleen desires sweetness, and the kidneys desire salt—these five flavors correspond to the qi of the five organs. If the organs are heated, the tongue develops sores, and the lips are revealed and red; if the bowels are cold, the tongue's base retracts, and the mouth is tight with blue lips. Cold should be supplemented, heat should be drained; when neither cold nor heat is present, adjustments should be made based on the organs. If the tongue retracts and the mouth is tight with blue lips, Sheng Ma Decoction is the proper treatment.[9p]

    　　　　疮疡全书 【金　窦汉卿】

    　　　　　木舌

    　　其木舌硬如穿山甲，外证憎寒壮热，语言蹇濇，此心经受热也。心者舌之本，因心而病，治法以小刀点紫黑处，煎药内多加山栀。山栀，泻火之要品也。
    　　　　　重舌

    　　其舌下生一小舌，其色鲜红，其外证颏下浮肿有硬核，此心经受热，毒气出于舌下。先用紫雪掺上，流出热涎；急服甘桔扬，加姜、灯心煎服。
    　　　　　重腭

    　　舌上生一疮，其状若杨梅，外证无寒无热，但作事烦心。先以甘桔汤多加山栀，后服黄连解毒汤，再吹冰片散；不宜用刀。
    　　　　　生疮

    　　舌生疮如黄栗，外证怯寒口张。先用蚌水，或田螺水，或苦茶缴净，然后搽药；次服鼠粘子解毒汤加山栀、黄连。口臭，冰片吹药内，加人中白、枯矾、铜青、黄连末。[10p]

    Complete Book of Sores and Ulcers 【Jin - Dou Hanqing】

    Wooden Tongue

    If the tongue is hard like that of a pangolin, the external signs exhibit aversion to cold and strong heat, with speech being hindered and sluggish; this indicates that the heart has endured heat. The heart is the root of the tongue; the disease arises from the heart. The treatment method involves using a small knife to prick the purple-black areas and decocting medicine with more gardenia fruit added. Gardenia is essential for clearing heat.

    Heavy Tongue

    If a small tongue grows underneath, its color bright red, with the external sign of swelling and a hard nodule below the chin; this indicates that the heart suffers from heat, and toxic energy emerges under the tongue. First, use purple snow powder to help release hot saliva; urgently consume sweet tangerine with added ginger and light heart in decoction.

    Heavy Palate

    If a sore forms on the tongue resembling a bayberry, with no signs of cold or heat but causing frustration; first use sweet tangerine soup with added gardenia, followed by administering the Coptis detoxifying soup, and then apply ice powder incense; it is inadvisable to use a knife.

    Tongue Sore

    If a sore appears on the tongue like a yellow chestnut, with an external sign of aversion to cold and open mouth; first use clam water, or freshwater snail water, or bitter tea to cleanse, then apply medicine; afterward, take a mouse glue detoxifying soup with added gardenia and Coptis. If there is bad breath, blow in ice powder medicine, adding borneol, burnt alunite, copper green, and powdered Coptis.[10p]

    　　　　　莲花舌

    　　舌下生三小舌，其类如莲花状。但舌乃心之苗，心火上炎，或思虑太过，或火气所伤，或酒后当风取凉，以致风痰相搏而成，此证急用清凉解毒汤加减服之，再吹冰片散；如肿不散，次用小刀针出紫血为妙。
    　　　　明理论 【金　成无己】

    　　　　　胎色

    　　舌者，心之官，法应南方。火本红而泽。伤寒三四日已后，舌上有膜白滑如胎，甚者或燥，或濇，或黄，或黑，是数者热气浅深之谓也。邪气在表者，舌上则无胎。及邪气传里，津液结搏，则舌上生胎也。寒邪初传，未全成热，或在半表，或在半里，或邪气客于胸中者，皆舌上胎白而滑也。经曰：舌上如胎者，以丹田有热，胸中有寒，邪初传入里者也。阳明病胁下鞕满，不大便而呕，舌上白胎者，可与小柴胡汤，是邪气在半表半里者也。阳明病若下之，则胃中空虚，客气动膈，心中懊憹，舌上胎者，栀子豉汤主之，是邪客于胸中者也。[11p]

    Lotus Flower Tongue

    Beneath the tongue are three small sub-tongues, resembling the shape of a lotus flower. However, the tongue is also a sprout of the heart. When the heart fire rises, it may result from excessive thinking, being harmed by fire, or taking cool air after drinking, which leads to wind-phlegm clashing and forming. For this condition, it is urgently advised to use a cooling detoxifying decoction with adjustments, and additionally apply powdered borneol. If swelling does not subside, it is advisable to use a small knife or needle to release purple blood.

    Fetal Color

    The tongue is the official of the heart and should correspond to the southern direction. Fire is inherently red and moist. After three to four days of cold damage, a membrane may appear on the tongue, white and slippery like that of a fetus. In severe cases, it may be dry, or have a yellow or black appearance, indicating varying depths of heat. If the evil qi is on the surface, the tongue will not show a membrane. However, when the evil qi penetrates inward and bodily fluids become obstructed, a membrane will form on the tongue. When cold evil first invades, the heat may not yet be fully formed, which may present as either a partial exterior or interior condition, or if the evil qi resides in the chest, the tongue will show a white and slippery membrane. The classics say: "A tongue that appears like a fetus indicates heat in the elixir field and cold in the chest, signifying the initial invasion of evil qi into the interior." In cases of Yangming disease with fullness under the ribs, constipation leading to vomiting, a white membranous tongue indicates that evil qi remains at the half surface and half interior. If Yangming disease is treated with purging, this may leave the stomach void, causing external qi to disturb the diaphragm, resulting in agitation in the heart. In such cases, a membranous tongue calls for the use of gardenia and fermented soy extract soup, indicating that evil qi resides in the chest.[11p]

    脏结宜若可下，舌上胎滑者，则云不可攻也，是邪未全成，热犹带表寒故也。及其邪传为热，则舌之胎不滑而濇也。经曰：伤寒七八日不解，热结在里，表里俱热，时时恶风，大渴，舌上干燥而烦，欲饮水数升者，白虎加人参汤主之。是热耗津液，而滑者已干也。若热聚于胃，则舌为之黄，是热已深也。《金匮要略》曰：舌黄，未下者，下之黄自去。若舌上色黑者，又为热之极也。《黄帝针经》曰：热病，口干舌黑者死。以心为君主之官，开窍于舌，黑为肾色，见于心部。心者，火，肾者，水。邪热已极，鬼贼相刑，故知必死。观其口舌，亦可见其逆顺矣。[12p]

    If there are dirty blockages that can be purged, and the tongue has a smooth coating, it is said that one should not attack, as the evil is not yet fully formed and the heat is still accompanied by cold. When the evil transforms into heat, the coating on the tongue becomes dry and rough. The classics state: If a febrile illness does not resolve after seven or eight days, it indicates that heat is locked inside, with both exterior and interior presenting heat, accompanied by intermittent chills, severe thirst, and a dry, vexed tongue, with a desire to drink several liters of water, the remedy is Baihu Jiajinshen Decoction. This heat depletes body fluids, and the smoothness has already dried up. If heat accumulates in the stomach, the tongue will turn yellow, indicating that the heat has penetrated deeply. The "Shanghan Lun" states: If the tongue is yellow and yet remains untreated, purging will cause the yellow to disappear. If the tongue is black, it indicates extreme heat. The "Huangdi Neijing" states: In heat illnesses, a dry mouth and a black tongue lead to death. The heart is regarded as the monarch, opening its orifices in the tongue. Black corresponds to the color of the kidney, reflected in the heart region. The heart symbolizes fire, while the kidney symbolizes water. When the evil heat reaches its extreme, it is a dire condition, indicating certain death. Observing the tongue and mouth also reveals the state of disorder or harmony within.[12p]

    　　　　儒门事亲 【元　张从政】

    　　　　　舌说

    　　热结于舌下，复生一小舌子，名曰子舌胀；热结于舌中，舌为之肿，名曰木舌胀。木者，强而不柔和也。微者可以咸软之，而大者以辛散之。昔尝治一妇人木舌胀，其舌满口，诸药不愈，余以(釒非)针小而锐者砭之，五七度肿减，三日方平，计所出血几至盈斗。
    　　　　东垣十书 【元　李杲】

    　　　　　生刺

    　　舌燥濇如杨梅刺者，生姜切厚片，蘸蜜于舌上揩之，其刺立消，神效。
    　　　　丹溪心法 【元　朱震亨】

    　　　　　肿胀

    　　木舌者，舌肿硬不和软也，百草霜、芒硝、滑石为末，酒调敷之。　　诸般舌肿胀，取龙脑破毒散半钱，以指蘸药擦舌上下，咽津下。[13p]

    The Confucian Approach to Filial Piety 【Yuan Dynasty, Zhang Congzheng】

    On Tongue Disorders

    Heat manifests under the tongue, resulting in a small growth known as "child tongue swelling"; when heat is present within the tongue, the tongue becomes swollen, referred to as "wooden tongue swelling." The term "wood" implies strength without gentleness. Minor cases can be softened, while severe cases require a pungent remedy. Once, I treated a woman with wooden tongue swelling; her tongue filled her mouth, and various medicines did not help. I used a small, sharp needle to puncture it, and after five to seven punctures, the swelling reduced. It took three days for the swelling to fully subside, with the blood loss amounting to nearly a bucket.

    Ten Writings of Dongyuan 【Yuan Dynasty, Li Gao】

    On Tongue Pain

    If the tongue feels dry and prickly like a bayberry thorn, slice fresh ginger into thick pieces, dip it in honey, and rub it on the tongue. The discomfort will vanish immediately, proving to be effective.

    Danxi's Heart Methods 【Yuan Dynasty, Zhu Zhenheng**

    On Swelling

    A wooden tongue refers to a tongue that is swollen, hard, and lacks softness. Use powdered herb frost, mirabilite, and talc as a mixture and apply it with wine. For various types of tongue swelling, take half a coin’s worth of dragon brain powder, dip a finger in, and rub the medicine on the tongue, both above and below, and swallow saliva down.[13p]

    　　　　　生疮

    　　舌上生疮，皆上焦热壅所致，宜如圣汤或甘桔汤加黄芩一钱，仍用柳花散掺之，或用白荷花瓣贴之。
    　　　　世医得效方 【元　危亦林】

    　　　　　口舌主五味

    　　心气通于舌，能知五味；脾气通于口，能知五谷。
    　　　　　舌之病能

    　　舌为心之官，主尝五味，以布五脏焉。　　心之本脉系于舌根，脾之络脉系于舌旁，肝脉循阴器络于舌本，肾之津液出于舌端，分布五脏，心实主之。三经为四气所中，则舌卷不能言；七情气郁，则舌肿不能语，至如心热则舌破生疮，肝壅则出血如涌，脾闭则白胎如雪。此舌之为病也。　　心气通于舌，心和故能知五味，脾气通于口，脾和故亦能知五谷之味。
    　　　　　重舌

    　　重舌先以凉水灌漱，次嚼生薄荷五七叶，却用如圣胜金锭一锭同嚼极烂，井水咽下，甚者连进三服，并以一锭安患处，其病随药便消。[14p]

    Sores on the Tongue

    Sores on the tongue are caused by heat and obstruction in the upper body. It is advisable to use the Holy Decoction or Sweet Tangerine Decoction with ten qian of Scutellaria, and mix in Willow Flower Powder, or apply white lotus petals.

    The Tongue and the Five Tastes

    The heart's energy connects to the tongue, enabling it to discern the five tastes; the spleen's energy connects to the mouth, allowing it to recognize the flavors of the five grains.

    Tongue Disorders

    The tongue is the organ of the heart, responsible for tasting the five flavors and distributing them to the five organs. The heart's main vessel is connected to the root of the tongue, while the spleen's network connects to the sides of the tongue. The liver's vessels circulate through the tongue's base, and the kidneys' fluids come out at the tongue's tip, distributing to the five organs, under the heart's control. If the three meridians are affected by the four Qi, the tongue may curl and be unable to speak; if the seven emotions are stagnant, the tongue may swell and be unable to articulate. For instance, if heat in the heart causes the tongue to ulcerate, obstruction in the liver may lead to bleeding like a surge, and blockage in the spleen may cause a white coating reminiscent of snow. These are the disorders of the tongue. The heart's energy connects to the tongue, and harmony in the heart enables the discernment of five tastes; the spleen's energy connects to the mouth, and harmony in the spleen allows for the recognition of the flavors of grains.

    Heavy Tongue

    For a heavy tongue, first rinse with cool water, then chew fresh peppermint leaves (five to seven leaves), followed by thoroughly chewing a piece of the Holy Golden Essence until it is extremely fine, then swallow with well water. In severe cases, take three doses continuously, and place a piece directly on the affected area; the illness will dissipate along with the medicine.[14p]

    　　　　　舌烂

    　　舌本烂，热不止者，逆。

    　　　　证治要诀 【明　戴思恭】

    　　　　　证治

    　　曾有舌上病疮，久蚀成穴，累服凉剂不效。后来有教服黑锡丹，遂得渐愈。此亦下虚，故上盛也。　　外有舌暴肿胀，名曰重舌，一味真蒲黄末掺之。　　又有舌无故常自痹者，不可作风治，由心血不足，理中汤加熟附子半钱，当归钱半。
    　　　　医学入门 【明　李梴】

    　　　　　舌属五脏

    　　心之本脉系于舌根，脾之络脉系于舌两旁，肝脉循阴器络于舌本，肾之津液出于舌端，分布五脏，心实主之。故曰：诸经皆会于口。
    　　　　　短强

    　　卒中风则舌短而强，舌卷不言者死。大概风用小续命汤，寒用理中汤，热用甘桔汤加防风、枳壳、黄芩。风寒湿舌强者，用白矾、肉桂末等分，安舌下，或正舌药。痰热舌强，壅肿或短，甘露饮。[15p]

    Tongue Ulcers

    If the tongue is rotten at its base and heat persists, it is a sign of rebellion.

    Key Points for Diagnosis and Treatment
    In the past, there were cases of ulcerated sores on the tongue that developed into cavities over time, and repeated use of cooling agents was ineffective. Eventually, the administration of Heixi Dan led to gradual recovery. This condition stems from deficiency below, thus leading to excess above. Additionally, if there is external swelling of the tongue, it is referred to as "heavy tongue," treated with a powder of true Puhuang. There are also cases where the tongue is inexplicably numb, which should not be treated as wind; instead, it is due to insufficient heart blood and can be addressed with a modified Lizhong Decoction by adding half a qian of熟附子 (prepared Aconite) and half a qian of Angelica.

    Introduction to Medicine
    The connection of the five organs to the tongue is as follows: the heart's primary vessels are attached at the root of the tongue, the spleen's collateral vessels are connected to the sides of the tongue, the liver's vessels run along the yin organs and connect at the base of the tongue, and the kidney’s fluids emerge at the tip of the tongue, distributing moisture to the five organs, with the heart primarily governing this. Thus, it is said: all channels converge at the mouth.

    Shortness and Rigidity of the Tongue
    In cases of sudden stroke, the tongue becomes short and rigid; if it curls and speech is lost, the patient may be near death. Generally, when there is wind, one uses the Xiao Xun Ming Decoction; for cold, the Lizhong Decoction; and for heat, a Sweet Tangerine Decoction with additional Fangfeng, Zhuhe, and Huangqin. If the tongue is stiff due to wind, cold, and dampness, use equal parts of alum and cinnamon powder to stabilize the tongue, or apply proper tongue medication. For a stiff tongue due to phlegm heat, which may also be swollen or shortened, use the Ganlu Drink.[15p]

    　　　　　肿长

    　　内因七情气郁，肿满不得息者，金沸草散。久不愈者，黑参丸，外用古霜盐散。因怒者，锈铁粉涂之。　　舌肿满口，气不得吐，名木舌。用陈茶、陈白梅，入巴豆七枚，同捣膏，薄荷水调刷口中，得下咽片时，即下一二行，以粥补住。如生疮连腮颊肿者，元参升麻汤。　　舌肿满口，不能声，饮食不通者，名重舌，用蒲黄频刷舌上自退。如不能咽药，即以黄连浓煎，时时呷之，以泻心火。　　舌肿如猪胞者，以针刺舌下两旁大脉，血出即消。切勿刺中脉，令血不止。悞刺，以火烧铜箸烙之，血再不止者死。或酢调锅煤，敷舌上下，脱去再敷，须臾自消。不食者亦死。　　舌肿，舌下有虫如蝼蛄、卧蚕，头小白，有尾，可烧铁烙，烙舌头上即消。　　舌长过寸者，单冰片末敷之。[16p]

    Swelling of the Tongue

    If the swelling is due to emotional factors causing stagnation of Qi, use Jin Fei Cao San. If it does not heal after a long time, apply Hei Shen Wan externally with ancient frost salt. If caused by anger, apply rusted iron powder.

    For a swollen tongue, making it hard to expel air, it is referred to as "wood tongue." Use aged tea and aged white plum, combined with seven Bajiao beans, pound them into a paste, rinse the mouth with mint water, and as soon as it is possible to swallow, take one or two pieces and supplement with congee. If there are sores connected to swelling of the cheeks, use Yuan Shen Sheng Ma Tang.

    For a swollen tongue that cannot produce sound and impedes food intake, known as "heavy tongue," continuously brush the tongue with catkins to help it reduce. If one cannot swallow medicine, take concentrated huanglian decoction and sip it frequently to clear heart fire.

    If the tongue is swollen like a pig's bladder, pierce the large veins on both sides under the tongue; when the blood flows out, the swelling will subside. Be careful not to pierce the veins themselves, which could cause continuous bleeding. Cauterize with a copper chopstick heated by fire; if bleeding does not stop, it could be fatal. Alternatively, mix vinegar with charcoal and apply it to both sides of the tongue; remove and reapply until it naturally subsides. If one refuses to eat, it could also be fatal.

    If the tongue is swollen and there are insects underneath resembling cricket or silkworm, small white head with a tail, it can be cauterized with hot iron directly on the tongue to make it disappear.

    If the tongue extends beyond an inch, apply powdered Bingshen (borax) to it.[16p]

    　　　　　破裂

    　　心热，生疮破裂，单黄连汤。脾热，兼舌胎干濇如雪，薄荷蜜冰蘗丸。心脾热，升麻葛根汤加薄荷、黄芩、桔梗。
    　　　　　胎色

    　　舌为心苗，肾主津液，无病则舌红而润，偶见红心点者，将欲发黄。如丹田邪热，则心苗枯槁，生胎如白胎然，是以邪在表则无胎，邪初传里则胎白而滑，胃寒热懊憹者，栀豉汤吐之。阳明病胁硬不大便而呕，舌胎白者，亦不可攻，小柴胡和之。如恶寒欲呕痰者，小柴胡加干姜。白胎滑而下利者，为脏结，不治。　　热渐入深则胎白而濇，热深入胃则胎黄，或肥光，或尖白根黄者，表多里少也，俱白虎加人参汤主之。　　手足腋下汗出，讝语便闭，胎紫带黑，或生芒刺，虫碎燥裂者，承气汤下之。[17p]

    Rupture

    Heart heat causes sores to rupture; use a simple Huanglian decoction. Spleen heat, accompanied by a dry, white tongue coating; use peppermint honey ice pill. For heart and spleen heat, use Shengma and Gegen decoction with additions of peppermint, Huangqin, and Jiegang.

    Fetal Color

    The tongue represents the heart's sprout, and the kidneys govern bodily fluids. When healthy, the tongue is red and moist; occasional red spots on the tongue indicate impending yellowing. If there is evildoing heat in the lower abdomen, the heart's sprout becomes withered, leading to a pale appearance akin to a white fetus. Thus, when evil is on the surface, there is no fetus; when it first penetrates inward, the fetus is pale and slippery. If there are symptoms of cold and heat in the stomach, use Zhizhi decoction to expel it. For Yangming disease with a hard side, constipation, and vomiting, where the tongue coating is white, do not forcefully purge; use Xiao Chaihu decoction to harmonize. If there is aversion to cold and the desire to vomit phlegm, add dried ginger to Xiao Chaihu. A slippery white fetus with diarrhea indicates internal stagnation, which should not be treated. As heat deepens, the fetus becomes white and dry; if heat deeply enters the stomach, the fetus becomes yellow, either plump and shiny or sharply white with a yellow root, suggesting an external excess with internal deficiency. Both require Baihu decoction with ginseng. Sweating in the hands, feet, and underarms, irregular speech, constipation, and a fetus appearing purple or black, or presenting with spikes or insect-like dry cracks, should be treated with Chengqi decoction.[17p]

    但舌黑亦有数种，有四边红而中灰黑成路者，失下也；有黑圈者，过经未解也；有黑尖者，虚烦也；有舌见黄而中有黑，至尖或乱黑点者，热毒深也；有弦红心黑，或白胎中见黑点者，表未解也；有根黑尖黄，脉滑者可下，脉浮者可汗；有尖黑而有乱纹脉滑实者，急下之。脉数无力者，必发渴而死。　　凡舌黑不论多少，俱系危证。惟冷而滑，如淡黑然者，乃无根虚火，可以化痰降火药治之。　　阴证胎白，腹痛自利者，理中汤。中湿湿痹，舌上如胎，非真胎也。丹田有热，胃中有寒，五苓散。　　外感风寒传经者，则舌胎自白而黄而黑者，死。[18p]

    There are several types of black tongues. A tongue that is red at the edges and gray-black in the center indicates a loss of fluids. A tongue with a black ring signifies unresolved pathogens. A tongue with a black tip indicates internal distress. If the tongue shows yellow with black in the middle and either a black tip or irregular black spots, it indicates deep heat toxicity. A tongue with red stripes and a black center, or black spots within a white coating, suggests unresolved exterior pathogens. A tongue with a black root and a yellow tip, accompanied by a slippery pulse, may indicate that it can be purged; if the pulse is floating, it can indicate sweating. A tongue that is sharply black with irregular lines and a slippery yet solid pulse requires urgent purging. If the pulse is rapid and weak, there will surely be thirst leading to death.

    In general, regardless of the degree of blackness, a black tongue all indicates a dangerous condition. Only if it is cold and slippery, resembling a pale black, does it signify rootless false heat, which can be treated with medicines to transform phlegm and reduce heat.

    For conditions of yin with a white coating on the tongue and abdominal pain with diarrhea, use the Li Zhong Tang. If there is dampness resulting in bi syndrome and the tongue resembles a coating, it is not genuine. For heat in the lower abdomen and cold in the stomach, use Wu Ling San.

    If there is an external wind-cold invading the channels, the tongue coating may be white, yellow, and black; this is a sign of death.[18p]

    　　　　医学纲目 【明　楼英】

    　　　　　舌属心脾

    　　舌属心脾。经云：心主舌。又云：在脏为心，在窍为舌。又云：心气通于舌，心和则舌能知五味。是舌属心也。又云：中央黄色，入通于脾，开窍于口，藏精于脾，故病在舌本。属脾也。
    　　　　　重舌

    　　舌根下生形如舌而小者，曰重舌；其着颊里及上腭者，曰重腭；其着齿龈上者，曰重龈。皆刺之，去血可也。
    　　　　　木舌

    　　木舌者，舌肿粗大，渐渐肿硬满口，不急治，即塞杀人也。其法用紫雪二钱，竹沥和匀，频抹口中，自消。[19p]

    Medical Guidelines 【Ming Dynasty, Lou Ying】

    Tongue Related to Heart and Spleen

    The tongue is associated with the heart and spleen. The classics say: the heart governs the tongue. It is also stated: in organs it is the heart, in orifices it is the tongue. Furthermore, it is said: the heart's energy flows to the tongue; when the heart is harmonious, the tongue can discern the five tastes. Thus, the tongue is related to the heart. Additionally, the central area is yellow, connected to the spleen, opening at the mouth, and storing essence in the spleen, hence diseases at the base of the tongue are related to the spleen.

    Heavy Tongue

    A small structure resembling the tongue that grows under the root of the tongue is called a heavy tongue; if it is attached inside the cheek or to the hard palate, it is called a heavy palate; if it is attached above the gums, it is called a heavy gum. All these should be pricked, and blood can be removed.

    Wooden Tongue

    A wooden tongue refers to a tongue that is swollen, thick, and gradually hardens, filling the mouth. If not treated promptly, it may lead to death. The method is to use two qian of purple snow, mixed with bamboo juice, to frequently apply in the mouth to resolve the condition.[19p]

    　　　　口齿类要 【明　薛己】

    　　　　　论证

    　　经言：舌乃心之苗。此以窍言也。以部分言之，五脏皆有所属；以证言之，五脏皆有所主。如口舌肿痛，或状如无皮，或发热作渴，为中气虚热；若眼如烟触，体倦少食，或午后益甚，为阴血虚热；若咽痛舌疮，口干足热，日哺益甚，为肾经虚火；若四肢逆冷，恶寒饮食，或痰甚眼赤，为命门火衰；若发热作渴，饮冷便闭，为脾胃实火；若发热恶寒，口干口渴，食少体倦，为脾经虚热；若舌本作强，腮颊肿痛，为脾经湿热；若痰盛作渴，口舌肿痛，为上焦有热；若思虑过度，口舌生疮，咽喉不利，为脾经血伤火动；若恚怒过度，寒热口苦而舌肿痛，为肝经血伤火动。病因多端，当因时制宜。凡舌肿胀甚，宜先刺舌尖，或舌上或边旁，出血泄毒，以救其急。惟舌下廉泉穴，此属肾经，虽宜出血，亦当禁针。[20p]

    Discussion on Oral and Pharyngeal Issues

    It is said: the tongue is a seed of the heart. This is expressed through obscure words. Speaking partially, each of the five organs has its corresponding aspect; when discussing in depth, each organ has its own master. For instance, if there is swelling and pain in the mouth and tongue, or if it appears as if there is no skin, or if there are symptoms of fever and thirst, this indicates a deficiency of central energy with heat. If the eyes appear smoky, the body feels fatigued with little appetite, or if symptoms worsen in the afternoon, this points to deficiency of yin and blood with heat. If there is throat pain, tongue sores, dry mouth, and significant heat in the feet, during the day it worsens, this indicates deficiency fire in the kidney channel. If the limbs feel cold and there is aversion to eating, or if phlegm is heavy and eyes are red, this suggests decline of fire at the gate of life. If there is fever and thirst, drinking cold beverages leads to constipation, this is indicative of excess fire in the spleen and stomach. If there is fever and chills, dry mouth and thirst, little food intake, and fatigue, this indicates deficiency heat in the spleen channel. If the tongue root is strong and there is swelling and pain in the cheeks and jaw, this signifies damp heat in the spleen channel. If phlegm is abundant causing thirst, with swelling and pain in the mouth and tongue, this shows heat in the upper burner. If there are excessive thoughts leading to sores in the mouth and tongue, and discomfort in the throat, this reflects injury to the blood of the spleen channel causing fire to stir. If there is excessive anger, with a bitter feeling in the mouth and swollen tongue, this indicates injury to the blood of the liver channel causing fire to stir. The causes of disease are numerous, requiring appropriate responses based on the time. In cases of severe tongue swelling, it is advisable to first prick the tip of the tongue, or the top or sides, to cause bleeding and release toxins, thus alleviating the urgency. However, for the sublingual area of the kidney channel, while it may be beneficial to release blood, acupuncture should be avoided.[20p]

    　　　　　验证舌法

    　　　　　　白胎舌
    　　见图
    　　舌见白胎滑者，邪初入里也。丹田有热，胸中有寒，乃少阳半表半里之证也。宜用小柴胡汤、栀子豉汤治之。
    　　　　　　将瘟舌
    　　见图
    　　舌见红色，热蓄于内也。不问何经，宜用透顶清神散治之。
    　　　　　　中焙舌
    　　见图
    　　舌见纯红，内有黑形如小舌者，乃邪热结于里也。君火炽盛，反兼水化。宜凉隔散、大柴胡汤下之。
    　　　　　　生斑舌
    　　见图
    　　舌见红色，而有小黑点者，热毒乘虚入胃，蓄热则发斑矣。宜用元参升麻葛根汤、化斑汤解之。
    　　　　　　红星舌[21p]

    Verification of Tongue Examination

    White Coated Tongue
    Upon observation, if the tongue appears white and slippery, it indicates that pathogens have just begun to enter the interior. There is heat in the lower dantian and cold in the chest, suggesting a condition of lesser yang, partially exterior and partially interior. It is advisable to use Xiao Chai Hu Tang or Zhi Zi Chi Tang to treat this.

    Plague Tongue
    If the tongue appears red, it indicates that heat is accumulating internally. Regardless of which meridian, it is recommended to use Tou Ding Qing Shen San to treat this.

    Middle Roasted Tongue
    If the tongue appears completely red and has a black shape resembling a small tongue, it indicates that pathogenic heat has become lodged internally. The fire is raging, which improperly combines with the water transformation. It is advisable to use Liang Ge San or Da Chai Hu Tang for treatment.

    Spotted Tongue
    If the tongue appears red with small black dots, it indicates that heat toxins have entered the stomach through a weakened state, leading to the formation of spots due to accumulated heat. It is advisable to use Yuan Shen Sheng Ma Ge Gen Tang or Hua Ban Tang to resolve this.

    Red Star Tongue[21p]

    　　见图
    　　舌见淡红，中有大红星者，乃少阴君火热之盛也，所不盛者，假火势以侮脾土，将欲发黄之候也。宜用茵陈五苓散治之。
    　　　　　　黑尖舌
    　　见图
    　　舌见红色，尖见青黑者，水虚火实，肾热所致。宜用竹叶石膏汤治之。
    　　　　　　里圈舌
    　　见图
    　　舌见淡红色，而中有一红晕，沿皆纯黑，乃余毒遗于心络之间，与邪火郁结，二火亢极，故有是证也。以承气汤下之。
    　　　　　　人裂舌
    　　见图
    　　舌见红色，更有裂纹如人字形者，乃君火燔灼，热毒炎上，故发裂也。宜用凉膈散。
    　　　　　　虫碎舌
    　　见图
    　　舌见红色，更有红点如虫蚀之状者，乃热毒炽甚，火在上，水在下，不能相济故也。宜用小承气汤下之。
    　　　　　　里黑舌
    　　见图
    　　舌见红色，内有干硬黑色，形如小长舌有刺者。此热毒炽甚，坚结大肠，金受火制，不能平木故也。急用调胃承气汤下之。
    　　　　　　厥阴舌
    　　见图[22p]

    • Light Red Tongue: When the tongue appears light red with a large red spot, this indicates an excess of the Yin Fire of the Lesser Yin. What is not excessive indicates a false fire wounding the Spleen Earth, resembling the impending signs of jaundice. It is advisable to use Yin Chen Wu Ling San for treatment.

    • Black Tipped Tongue: When the tongue appears red with a bluish-black tip, this indicates deficiency of Water and excess of Fire, caused by Kidney Heat. It is advisable to use Bamboo Leaf and Gypsum Decoction for treatment.

    • Ringed Tongue: When the tongue is light red with a red halo in the center and pure black around the edges, this indicates residual toxins left in the Heart's network, along with obstructed evil fire. The two fires are excessively elevated, resulting in this symptom. It is recommended to use Cheng Qi Tang to purge it.

    • Cracked Tongue: When the tongue appears red with cracks resembling a person character, this indicates burning fire and toxic heat rising, causing the cracks. It is advisable to use Liang Ge San for treatment.

    • Insect Fractured Tongue: When the tongue is red with red spots resembling insect bites, this indicates extreme toxic heat; fire is above and water is below, unable to support each other. It is advisable to use Xiao Cheng Qi Tang to purge it.

    • Inner Black Tongue: When the tongue is red, with dry hard black inside, resembling a small long tongue with spikes, this indicates extreme toxic heat, solidifying the large intestine. Metal is restrained by Fire, unable to balance Wood. It is urgent to use Tiao Wei Cheng Qi Tang to purge it.

    • Jueyin Tongue: [Image reference not provided for translation.][22p]

    　　舌见红色，内有黑纹者，乃阴毒厥于肝经。肝主筋，故舌见如丝形也。用理中合四逆汤温之。
    　　　　　　死现舌
    　　见图
    　　舌见黑色，水克火明矣。患此者，百无一治。治者审之！
    　　　　　　黄胎舌
    　　见图
    　　舌见尖白根黄，其表证未罢也，须宜解表，然后方可攻之。如大便秘者，用凉膈散加硝黄泡服。小便濇者，用五苓散加木通，合益元散加姜汁少许，以白滚汤调服。
    　　　　　　黑心舌
    　　见图
    　　舌见弦白心黑而脉沉微者，难治；脉浮滑者可汗，沉实者可下。始病即发此色，乃危殆之甚也，速进调胃承气汤下之。
    　　　　　　十五舌
    　　见图
    　　舌尖白胎二分，根黑一分，必有身痛恶寒，如饮水不至，甚者五苓散；自汗，渴者白虎汤；下利者解毒汤。此亦危证也。
    　　　　　　十六舌
    　　见图
    　　舌见白胎，中有黑小点乱生者，尚有表证。其病之来虽恶，宜凉膈散微表之，表退即当下之。下用调胃承气汤。[23p]

    • A red tongue with black lines indicates a hidden toxin affecting the liver channel. The liver governs the tendons, hence the tongue appears thread-like. Treat it with the "Four Reverse Decoction" to warm.

      (See the image)
      A black tongue signifies water overcoming fire. Those suffering this condition have little chance of recovery. Treatment must be cautious!

      (See the image)
      A tongue with a white tip, a yellow root, signifies the exterior syndrome has not resolved; the exterior must be resolved before addressing further issues. For constipation, use "Cool the Stomach Powder" with a pinch of yellow nitrate; for frequent urination, use "Five-Ingredient Powder" with some Muxiang, combining with "Yiyuan Powder" and a little ginger juice, taken with hot water.

    • Black-hearted Tongue
      (See the image)
      A white-edged tongue with a black center and a weak pulse is hard to treat; with a floating and slippery pulse, sweating is possible, while a sinking and solid pulse can indicate a need for purging. The appearance of this color at the onset of illness indicates severe danger; promptly administer "Stomach Adjusting and Invigorating Decoction."

    • Fifteen Tongue
      (See the image)
      A tongue with a white tip, a black root, and a portion of the body in pain and chills, suggests severe issues like poor hydration, treated with "Five-Ingredient Powder." If there's sweating and thirst, use "White Tiger Decoction." If there's diarrhea, give "Detox Decoction." This too indicates a critical condition.

    • Sixteen Tongue

Although the illness may be serious, it is appropriate to use "Cool the Stomach Powder" to target the exterior. Once the exterior is resolved, then purging with "Stomach Adjusting and Invigorating Decoction" is advised.[23p]

    　　　　　　十七舌

    　　　　　　二十一舌

    Seventeenth Tongue

    As observed in the illustration, the tongue appears gray with two black rings in the center. This indicates heat affecting the kidneys and the Mingmen. It is advisable to purge urgently by administering a detoxifying decoction three to five times; otherwise, treatment may become difficult if delayed. Initially, a greater quantity of rhubarb soaked in wine should be used.

    Eighteenth Tongue

    As observed in the illustration, the tongue shows a slight yellow color. If this is noted at the onset of illness with speech disturbances, it indicates that exterior pathogens have penetrated inward due to loss of sweating. Sweating and purging both need to be applied. The treatment should incorporate a formula combining detoxifying decoction with an antitoxic powder.

    Nineteenth Tongue

    As observed in the illustration, the tongue has a white coating with slight yellow. This indicates impending diarrhea, and it is advisable to take a detoxifying decoction; if there is aversion to cold, use the Wuling powder.

    Twentieth Tongue

    As observed in the illustration, the tongue shows a slight yellow color. This suggests that the exterior symptoms have not yet resolved. It is recommended to use Xiaochaihu Decoction combined with Tianshui powder. If purging is appropriate, use Dazhao Hu Decoction to eliminate both exterior and interior pathogens, applying it judiciously in clinical practice.

    Twenty-First Tongue

    As observed in the illustration, the tongue appears yellow, indicating that a previously white coating has changed to yellow. This signifies that heat has entered the stomach from the exterior, and urgent purging is required. If purging is delayed, it may turn black, resulting in a severe condition that indicates extreme internal damage. A detoxifying formula should be utilized for purging.

    Twenty-Second Tongue

    As observed in the illustration, the tongue has a white coating on the left side with spontaneous sweating. In this case, do not purge. Instead, utilize Baihu Decoction supplemented with three qian of ginseng.[24p]

    Twenty-Third Tongue
    Refer to the illustration.
    If the right side of the tongue shows a white coat and is slick, this indicates a disease in the muscles, with the evil being at the surface and interior. It will surely lead to alternating cold and heat. It is advisable to use Xiao Chai Hu Decoction for harmonization.

    Twenty-Fourth Tongue
    Refer to the illustration.
    If the left side of the tongue shows a white coat and is slick, this signifies a condition of stasis in the internal organs, with the evil having invaded the organs, making it difficult to treat.

    Twenty-Fifth Tongue
    Refer to the illustration.
    If the tongue shows a white coat around the edges and yellow in the center, this must indicate symptoms of thirst and vomiting. If there are also surface symptoms, take Wu Ling San and Yi Yuan San together. Wait until the yellow disappears before proceeding with treatment.

    Twenty-Sixth Tongue
    Refer to the illustration.
    If the tongue shows yellow with small black dots, this indicates that the evil has spread through the six organs and is about to enter the five organs. It is urgent to take Tiao Wei Cheng Qi Decoction to purge it, and subsequently take a harmonizing powder, which can save one from critical conditions.

    Twenty-Seventh Tongue
    Refer to the illustration.
    If the tongue shows yellow with a pointed white appearance, this indicates that there is less symptom at the surface and more inside. It is advisable to take Tian Shui San once and Liang Ge San twice combined. If the pulse is wiry, it is best to use Fang Feng Tong Sheng San.

    Twenty-Eighth Tongue
    Refer to the illustration.
    If the tongue shows yellow with interspersed papules, this indicates that heat has entered the stomach, and the evil toxin is deep. Symptoms include heart fire and thirst; it is urgent to take Da Cheng Qi Decoction to purge it. If there is jaundice, use Yin Chen San; for blood in the stool, use Di Dang San; if there is water accumulation in the flanks, use Shi Zi San; for severe chest obstruction, use Da Xian Zhi Zhong Tang; for distention, use Da Huang Xie Xin Tang.[25p]

    　　　　　　二十九舌
    　　见图
    　　舌见四边微红，中间灰黑色者，此由失下而致。用大承气汤下之，热退可愈。必三四下方退。五次下之而不退者，不治。
    　　　　　　三十舌
    　　见图
    　　舌见黄而黑点乱生者，其证必渴，讝语，脉实者生，脉濇者死，循衣摸床者不治。若下之见黑粪，亦不治。下，宜大承气汤。
    　　　　　　三十一舌
    　　见图
    　　舌见黄中黑至尖者，热气已深，两感见之十当九死，恶寒甚者亦死，不恶寒而下利者可治。宜用调胃承气汤主之。
    　　　　　　三十二舌
    　　见图
    　　舌见外淡红心淡黑者，如恶风表未罢，用双解加解毒汤相半微汗之，汗罢急下之。如结胸，烦躁目直视者不治。非结胸者可治。
    　　　　　　三十三舌
    　　见图
    　　舌见灰色尖黄，不恶风寒脉浮者，可下之。若恶风恶寒者，用双解散加解毒汤主之。三四下之见粪黑，不治。[26p]

    Twenty-Ninth Tongue

    The tongue appears slightly red on the four edges and gray-black in the center; this results from deficiency. Administer a large number of purgative decoction, and recovery may occur once the heat subsides. It may require three or four doses to reduce. If after five doses the condition does not improve, it is incurable.

    Thirtieth Tongue

    The tongue displays yellow with chaotic black spots. The symptoms must include thirst and slurred speech; a strong pulse indicates life, while a weak pulse indicates death. Those who touch their clothes or feel around the bed are beyond treatment. If black feces are seen after purging, it is also incurable. A large purgative decoction is recommended.

    Thirty-First Tongue

    The tongue shows yellow with black reaching the tip, indicating deep heat. It is found in ten out of nine cases that such patients die. Severe chills also indicate death, while those without chills but having diarrhea may be treatable. Use a regulating stomach purgative decoction as the primary treatment.

    Thirty-Second Tongue

    The tongue presents a pale red exterior and a pale black center, resembling an ongoing response to a bad wind. Administer a modified detoxification decoction to induce slight sweating, and after sweating, promptly purge. If there's a sensation of constriction in the chest and restlessness with a fixed gaze, it is not treatable. Other cases may be treated.

    Thirty-Third Tongue

    The tongue shows a gray color with a yellow tip and does not react negatively to wind or cold, with a floating pulse, suitable for purging. If there is aversion to wind and cold, a modified detoxification decoction should be used. After three or four purges, if black feces are seen, it is incurable.[26p]

    　　　　　　三十四舌
    　　见图
    　　舌见灰黑色而有黑纹者，脉实，急用大承气汤下之；脉浮，渴饮水者，用凉膈散解之。十可救其二三。
    　　　　　　三十五舌

    　　舌根微黑尖黄，脉滑者可下之，脉浮者当养阴退阳。若恶风寒者微汗之，用双解散。若下利，用解毒汤，十生八九也。
    　　　　　　三十六舌
    　　见图
